<script>
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Configuration
// Panels register themselves — adding a new panel
// requires only: add nav-item, add panel div, add
// to PANELS registry, implement render function.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
const apiPort = params.get('api') || '3000';
const API = `http://localhost:${apiPort}/v1`;
const SIGNALS_URL = `http://localhost:${apiPort}/signals`;

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// State
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const State = {
  agent: null,
  connected: false,
  networkState: null,
  reputation: null,
  myManifests: [],
  eventCount: 0,
};

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// API
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const Api = {
  async get(path) {
    const res = await fetch(`${API}${path}`);
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`${res.status} ${path}`);
    return res.json();
  },
  async post(path, body) {
    const res = await fetch(`${API}${path}`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify(body),
    });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`${res.status} ${path}`);
    return res.json();
  },
};

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Router
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const Router = {
  current: 'monitor',
  navigate(panelId) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(n => n.classList.remove('active'));
    const panel = document.getElementById(`panel-${panelId}`);
    const navItem = document.querySelector(`[data-panel="${panelId}"]`);
    if (panel) panel.classList.add('active');
    if (navItem) navItem.classList.add('active');
    this.current = panelId;
    Panels[panelId]?.onActivate?.();
  },
};

document.getElementById('nav').addEventListener('click', e => {
  const item = e.target.closest('.nav-item');
  if (item?.dataset.panel) Router.navigate(item.dataset.panel);
});

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Utilities
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const fmt = {
  hash: h => h ? `${h.slice(0,8)}…${h.slice(-6)}` : '—',
  score: s => typeof s === 'number' ? s.toFixed(4) : '—',
  delta: d => {
    if (typeof d !== 'number') return '';
    return d >= 0 ? `↑${d.toFixed(3)}` : `↓${Math.abs(d).toFixed(3)}`;
  },
  time: () => new Date().toISOString().slice(11, 19),
  arch: a => a || '—',
  params: n => {
    if (!n) return '—';
    if (n >= 1e12) return (n/1e12).toFixed(1)+'T';
    if (n >= 1e9)  return (n/1e9).toFixed(1)+'B';
    if (n >= 1e6)  return (n/1e6).toFixed(1)+'M';
    return n.toString();
  },
};

function copyText(text) {
  navigator.clipboard?.writeText(text).then(() => {
    const el = document.querySelector('.agent-key');
    if (el) {
      const orig = el.textContent;
      el.textContent = 'copied';
      el.style.color = 'var(--accent)';
      setTimeout(() => {
        el.textContent = orig;
        el.style.color = '';
      }, 300);
    }
  });
}

function passes(score) { return typeof score === 'number' && score >= 0.618; }

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Panels registry
// To add a new panel: implement { onActivate, render }
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const Panels = {};

// ─── Monitor Panel ───────────────────────────────

let maxEvents = 200;

Panels.monitor = {
  onActivate() {},
  addEvent(type, hash, raw) {
    State.eventCount++;
    document.getElementById('sb-events').textContent = State.eventCount;

    const stream = document.getElementById('event-stream');
    const empty = stream.querySelector('.stream-empty');
    if (empty) empty.remove();

    const typeClass = {
      'ValidationRequested': 'validation',
      'QuorumReached':        'quorum',
      'AttestationCreated':   'attestation',
      'WarrantCreated':        'warrant',
      'ManifestCreated':       'manifest',
    }[type] || 'manifest';

    const typeLabel = {
      'ValidationRequested': 'VALIDATION.REQ',
      'QuorumReached':        'QUORUM.REACHED',
      'AttestationCreated':   'ATTESTATION',
      'WarrantCreated':        'WARRANT',
      'ManifestCreated':       'MANIFEST',
    }[type] || type;

    const row = document.createElement('div');
    row.className = 'event-row';
    row.innerHTML = `
      <span class="ev-time">${fmt.time()}</span>
      <span class="ev-type ${typeClass}">${typeLabel}</span>
      <span class="ev-hash">${hash || '—'}</span>
    `;

    stream.prepend(row);

    // Prune old events
    const rows = stream.querySelectorAll('.event-row');
    if (rows.length > maxEvents) rows[rows.length - 1].remove();
  },
};

// ─── Query Panel ─────────────────────────────────

Panels.query = {
  onActivate() {
    document.getElementById('search-input').focus();
  },
  async search(val) {
    const container = document.getElementById('query-result');
    container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty loading">querying</div>';

    try {
      if (val.startsWith('hCkk') || val.startsWith('hC')) {
        await this.renderManifest(container, val);
      } else if (val.startsWith('uhCAk') || val.startsWith('uhC')) {
        await this.renderAgent(container, val);
      } else if (val.startsWith('sha256:') || val.match(/^[a-f0-9]{64}$/)) {
        await this.renderConvergence(container, val);
      } else {
        container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">unrecognized format — enter manifest hash (hCkk...), agent pubkey (uhCAk...), or content hash (sha256:...)</div>';
      }
    } catch(e) {
      container.innerHTML = `<div class="empty">error: ${e.message}</div>`;
    }
  },

  async renderManifest(container, hash) {
    const entry_preview = await Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}`).catch(() => null);
    const contentHash = entry_preview?.entry?.content_hash;

    const [manifest, attestations, warrants, trustScore, upstreams, derivatives, convergenceHashes] = await Promise.all([
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}`),
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}/attestations`).catch(() => []),
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}/warrants`).catch(() => []),
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}/trust-score`).catch(() => null),
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}/upstreams`).catch(() => []),
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}/derivatives`).catch(() => []),
      contentHash ? Api.get(`/content/${encodeURIComponent(contentHash)}/manifests`).catch(() => []) : Promise.resolve([]),
    ]);

    const entry = manifest.entry || {};
    const score = trustScore?.score ?? 0;
    const pct = (score * 100).toFixed(1);
    const scoreClass = passes(score) ? 'accent' : 'warn';
    const warrantHtml = warrants.length > 0
      ? `<div class="warrant-banner">⚠ ${warrants.length} active warrant${warrants.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}</div>`
      : '';

    const attRows = (attestations || []).map(a => {
      const p = a.entry?.passed !== false;
      const sc = a.entry?.score != null ? Number(a.entry.score).toFixed(3) : '—';
      return `<div class="att-row">
        <div class="att-dot ${p ? 'pass' : 'fail'}"></div>
        <div class="att-agent hash" onclick="copyText('${a.author}')" title="${a.author}">${fmt.hash(a.author)}</div>
        <div class="att-score">${sc}</div>
        <div class="att-verdict ${p ? 'pass' : 'fail'}">${p ? 'pass' : 'fail'}</div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');

    const upstreamHtml = upstreams.length > 0
      ? upstreams.map(h => `<span class="lineage-hash" onclick="Panels.query.goHash('${h}')">${fmt.hash(h)}</span>`).join('')
      : '<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">none</span>';

    const derivHtml = derivatives.length > 0
      ? derivatives.map(h => `<span class="lineage-hash" onclick="Panels.query.goHash('${h}')">${fmt.hash(h)}</span>`).join('')
      : '<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">none</span>';

    container.innerHTML = `
      ${warrantHtml}
      <div class="query-result">
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header">
            <span class="rb-title">trust score</span>
            <span class="rb-value ${scoreClass}">${fmt.score(score)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="score-bar">
            <div class="score-fill ${passes(score) ? '' : 'warn'}" style="width:${pct}%"></div>
            <div class="score-threshold"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="kv-grid">
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">hash</div><div class="kv-val hash" onclick="copyText('${hash}')" title="${hash}">${fmt.hash(hash)}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">architecture</div><div class="kv-val">${fmt.arch(entry.architecture)}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">parameters</div><div class="kv-val">${fmt.params(entry.parameter_count)}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">version</div><div class="kv-val">${entry.version || '—'}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">source</div><div class="kv-val">${entry.connector_source || '—'}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">attestations</div><div class="kv-val ${attestations.length > 0 ? 'accent' : ''}">${attestations.length}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item" style="grid-column:1/-1"><div class="kv-key">description</div><div class="kv-val" style="white-space:normal">${entry.description || '—'}</div></div>
          </div>
        </div>

        ${attestations.length > 0 ? `
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header"><span class="rb-title">attestations</span></div>
          <div class="attestation-list">${attRows}</div>
        </div>` : ''}

        ${convergenceHashes.length > 1 ? `
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header">
            <span class="rb-title">convergence</span>
            <span class="rb-value accent">${convergenceHashes.length}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="lineage-section">
            <div class="lineage-label">independent registrations of same weights</div>
            <div>${convergenceHashes
              .filter(h => h !== hash)
              .map(h => `<span class="lineage-hash" onclick="Panels.query.goHash('${h}')">${fmt.hash(h)}</span>`)
              .join('')}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>` : ''}

        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header"><span class="rb-title">lineage</span></div>
          <div class="lineage-section">
            <div class="lineage-label">upstream</div>
            <div>${upstreamHtml}</div>
          </div>
          <div class="lineage-section" style="border-top:1px solid var(--border)">
            <div class="lineage-label">derivatives</div>
            <div>${derivHtml}</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  },

  async renderAgent(container, pubkey) {
    const [rep, manifests] = await Promise.all([
      Api.get(`/agent/${pubkey}/reputation`).catch(() => ({})),
      Api.get(`/agent/${pubkey}/manifests`).catch(() => []),
    ]);

    const deltaClass = rep.score_delta >= 0 ? 'up' : 'down';
    const manifestRows = manifests.map(m => {
      const e = m.entry || {};
      return `<div class="manifest-row" onclick="Panels.query.goHash('${m.hash}')">
        <div class="mr-hash hash">${fmt.hash(m.hash)} <span style="color:var(--text3)">${e.architecture || ''}</span></div>
        <div class="mr-arch">${fmt.params(e.parameter_count)}</div>
        <div class="mr-score">—</div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');

    container.innerHTML = `
      <div class="query-result">
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header">
            <span class="rb-title">agent</span>
            <span class="rb-value ${passes(rep.score) ? 'accent' : 'warn'}">${fmt.score(rep.score)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="kv-grid">
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">pubkey</div><div class="kv-val hash" onclick="copyText('${pubkey}')">${fmt.hash(pubkey)}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">trajectory</div><div class="kv-val ${deltaClass}">${fmt.delta(rep.score_delta)}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">attestations</div><div class="kv-val">${rep.attestation_count ?? 0}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">warrants</div><div class="kv-val ${rep.warrant_count > 0 ? 'warn' : ''}">${rep.warrant_count ?? 0}</div></div>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${manifests.length > 0 ? `
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header"><span class="rb-title">manifests (${manifests.length})</span></div>
          ${manifestRows}
        </div>` : ''}
      </div>
    `;
  },

  async renderConvergence(container, contentHash) {
    const hashes = await Api.get(`/content/${encodeURIComponent(contentHash)}/manifests`).catch(() => []);
    container.innerHTML = `
      <div class="query-result">
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header">
            <span class="rb-title">convergence</span>
            <span class="rb-value ${hashes.length > 1 ? 'accent' : 'neutral'}">${hashes.length}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="kv-grid">
            <div class="kv-item" style="grid-column:1/-1">
              <div class="kv-key">content hash</div>
              <div class="kv-val">${contentHash}</div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="lineage-section">
            <div class="lineage-label">independent registrations</div>
            <div>${hashes.length > 0
              ? hashes.map(h => `<span class="lineage-hash" onclick="Panels.query.goHash('${h}')">${fmt.hash(h)}</span>`).join('')
              : '<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">none found</span>'
            }</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  },

  goHash(hash) {
    document.getElementById('search-input').value = hash;
    this.search(hash);
  },
};

document.getElementById('search-input').addEventListener('keydown', e => {
  if (e.key === 'Enter') {
    const val = e.target.value.trim();
    if (val) Panels.query.search(val);
  }
});

// ─── Status Panel ────────────────────────────────

Panels.status = {
  async onActivate() { await this.render(); },
  async render() {
    if (!State.agent) return;
    const body = document.getElementById('status-body');

    const [rep, manifests, netState] = await Promise.all([
      Api.get(`/agent/${State.agent}/reputation`).catch(() => ({})),
      Api.get(`/agent/${State.agent}/manifests`).catch(() => []),
      Api.get('/network/state').catch(() => ({})),
    ]);

    State.reputation = rep;
    State.networkState = netState;
    State.myManifests = manifests;

    const deltaClass = (rep.score_delta || 0) >= 0 ? 'up' : 'down';
    const progress = netState.attestation_count
      ? netState.attestation_count / netState.next_fibonacci_threshold
      : 0;

    const phaseLabel = netState.phase === 0 ? 'GENESIS' : 'GOVERNED';
    const phaseClass = netState.phase === 0 ? 'genesis' : 'governed';

    const manifestRows = manifests.slice(0, 10).map(m => {
      const e = m.entry || {};
      return `<div class="manifest-row" onclick="Router.navigate('query');Panels.query.goHash('${m.hash}')">
        <div class="mr-hash">${fmt.hash(m.hash)} <span style="color:var(--text3)">${e.architecture || ''}</span></div>
        <div class="mr-arch">${fmt.params(e.parameter_count)}</div>
        <div class="mr-score">—</div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');

    body.innerHTML = `
      <div class="status-grid">
        <div class="stat-card">
          <div class="stat-label">reputation</div>
          <div class="stat-value ${passes(rep.score) ? 'accent' : 'warn'}">${fmt.score(rep.score)}</div>
          <div class="stat-sub ${deltaClass}">${fmt.delta(rep.score_delta)}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
          <div class="stat-label">attestations</div>
          <div class="stat-value">${rep.attestation_count ?? 0}</div>
          <div class="stat-sub">warrants: ${rep.warrant_count ?? 0}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
          <div class="stat-label">manifests</div>
          <div class="stat-value">${manifests.length}</div>
          <div class="stat-sub">${phaseClass === 'genesis' ? 'genesis phase' : 'governed phase'}</div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="fib-progress">
        <div class="fib-label">
          <span>fibonacci cycle ${netState.cycle ?? 0}</span>
          <span>${netState.attestation_count ?? 0} / ${netState.next_fibonacci_threshold ?? 21}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="fib-bar">
          <div class="fib-fill" style="width:${Math.min(100, progress * 100).toFixed(1)}%"></div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="section-head">agent</div>
      <div class="phi-table">
        <div class="phi-row">
          <span class="phi-name">pubkey</span>
          <span class="phi-val hash" onclick="copyText('${State.agent}')">${fmt.hash(State.agent)}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="phi-row">
          <span class="phi-name">credit supply</span>
          <span class="phi-val">${netState.credit_supply?.toLocaleString() ?? '—'}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="phi-row">
          <span class="phi-name">network phase</span>
          <span class="phi-val"><span class="phase-badge ${phaseClass}">${phaseLabel}</span></span>
        </div>
      </div>

      ${manifests.length > 0 ? `
      <div class="section-head">registered manifests</div>
      ${manifestRows}
      ` : ''}
    `;
  },
};

Panels.network = {
  async onActivate() { await this.render(); },
  async render() {
    const body = document.getElementById('network-body');
    const state = State.networkState || await Api.get('/network/state').catch(() => ({}));
    State.networkState = state;

    const progress = state.attestation_count
      ? state.attestation_count / state.next_fibonacci_threshold
      : 0;

    body.innerHTML = `
      <div class="status-grid" style="grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr 1fr 1fr">
        <div class="stat-card">
          <div class="stat-label">attestations</div>
          <div class="stat-value accent">${state.attestation_count ?? 0}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
          <div class="stat-label">credit supply</div>
          <div class="stat-value">${state.credit_supply?.toLocaleString() ?? '—'}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
          <div class="stat-label">next threshold</div>
          <div class="stat-value">${state.next_fibonacci_threshold ?? 21}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card">
          <div class="stat-label">cycle</div>
          <div class="stat-value">${state.cycle ?? 0}</div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="fib-progress">
        <div class="fib-label">
          <span>progress to next fibonacci threshold</span>
          <span>${(progress * 100).toFixed(1)}%</span>
        </div>
        <div class="fib-bar">
          <div class="fib-fill" style="width:${Math.min(100, progress * 100).toFixed(1)}%"></div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="section-head">φ-derived constants</div>
      <div class="phi-table">
        <div class="phi-row"><span class="phi-name">quorum threshold</span><span class="phi-val">total_rep / φ² = total / 2.618</span></div>
        <div class="phi-row"><span class="phi-name">pass threshold</span><span class="phi-val">φ⁻¹ = 0.618</span></div>
        <div class="phi-row"><span class="phi-name">admission gate closes</span><span class="phi-val">honest_rep &lt; φ⁻¹ = 0.618</span></div>
        <div class="phi-row"><span class="phi-name">reveal window opens</span><span class="phi-val">commit_weight ≥ total / φ⁴</span></div>
        <div class="phi-row"><span class="phi-name">reveal deadline</span><span class="phi-val">φ⁴ × 10s = 68.5s</span></div>
        <div class="phi-row"><span class="phi-name">credit expansion</span><span class="phi-val">supply × φ = supply × 1.618</span></div>
        <div class="phi-row"><span class="phi-name">new agent reputation</span><span class="phi-val">avg_rep / φ² = avg / 2.618</span></div>
        <div class="phi-row"><span class="phi-name">convergence score</span><span class="phi-val">1 − φ⁻ⁿ (n = registrations)</span></div>
        <div class="phi-row"><span class="phi-name">min validators</span><span class="phi-val">3</span></div>
        <div class="phi-row"><span class="phi-name">bootstrap threshold</span><span class="phi-val">21 attestations (fib)</span></div>
      </div>

      <div class="section-head">credit history</div>
      <div class="phi-table">
        <div class="phi-row" style="color:var(--text3);font-size:10px">
          <span>crossing → attestations → supply</span><span></span>
        </div>
        ${[
          [1,13,987],[2,21,1596],[3,34,2581],[4,55,4177],[5,89,6755]
        ].map(([c,a,s]) =>
          `<div class="phi-row">
            <span class="phi-name" style="color:var(--text3)">crossing ${c} · att ${a}</span>
            <span class="phi-val">${s.toLocaleString()}</span>
          </div>`
        ).join('')}
      </div>
    `;
  },
};

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Signal Stream
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

function connectSignals() {
  const es = new EventSource(SIGNALS_URL);

  es.onmessage = (event) => {
    try {
      const signal = JSON.parse(event.data);
      const payload = signal?.value?.payload || signal;
      const type = payload?.type;
      if (!type) return;

      const hash =
        payload.request_hash ||
        payload.quorum_bundle_hash ||
        payload.action_hash || '';

      Panels.monitor.addEvent(type, fmt.hash(hash), payload);

      // Refresh network state quietly
      if (type === 'AttestationCreated' || type === 'QuorumReached') {
        Api.get('/network/state').then(s => {
          State.networkState = s;
          updateStatusBar(s);
        }).catch(() => {});
      }
    } catch(e) {}
  };

  es.onopen = () => {
    State.connected = true;
    updateConnectionStatus(true);
  };

  es.onerror = () => {
    State.connected = false;
    updateConnectionStatus(false);
    es.close();
    setTimeout(connectSignals, 5000);
  };
}

function updateConnectionStatus(connected) {
  const dot = document.getElementById('conn-dot');
  const label = document.getElementById('conn-status');
  dot.className = `status-dot${connected ? '' : ' offline'}`;
  label.textContent = connected ? 'connected' : 'reconnecting';
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Status bar
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

function updateStatusBar(state) {
  if (!state) return;
  document.getElementById('sb-att').textContent = state.attestation_count ?? '—';
  document.getElementById('sb-threshold').textContent = state.next_fibonacci_threshold ?? '—';
  document.getElementById('sb-supply').textContent = state.credit_supply?.toLocaleString() ?? '—';
  document.getElementById('sb-phase').textContent = state.phase === 0 ? 'genesis' : 'governed';
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Clock
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

function updateClock() {
  document.getElementById('tb-time').textContent = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,19).replace('T', ' ') + 'Z';
}
updateClock();
setInterval(updateClock, 1000);

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Init
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

async function init() {
  // Agent identity
  try {
    const { agent } = await Api.get('/agent/me');
    State.agent = agent;
    const keyEl = document.getElementById('agent-key');
    keyEl.textContent = fmt.hash(agent);
    keyEl.title = agent;
    keyEl.onclick = () => copyText(agent);
  } catch(e) {}

  // Network state
  try {
    const state = await Api.get('/network/state');
    State.networkState = state;
    updateStatusBar(state);
  } catch(e) {}

  // Signals
  connectSignals();

  // Poll network state every 10s
  setInterval(async () => {
    try {
      const s = await Api.get('/network/state');
      State.networkState = s;
      updateStatusBar(s);
    } catch(e) {}
  }, 10000);
}

Panels.browse = {
  loaded: false,
  async onActivate() {
    if (!this.loaded) await this.render();
  },
  async render() {
    const body = document.getElementById('browse-body');
    body.innerHTML = '<div class="empty loading">fetching manifests</div>';
    try {
      const manifests = await Api.get('/manifests');
      if (!manifests.length) {
        body.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">no manifests registered yet</div>';
        return;
      }

      // Fetch registering agent reputations
      const agentReps = {};
      await Promise.all([...new Set(manifests.map(m => m.author))].map(async a => {
        try {
          const rep = await Api.get(`/agent/${a}/reputation`);
          agentReps[a] = rep.score ?? 0;
        } catch(e) { agentReps[a] = 0; }
      }));

      const rows = manifests.map((m, i) => {
        const e = m.entry || {};
        const agentRep = agentReps[m.author] ?? 0;
        const scoreClass = m.passes ? 'pass' : '';
        const rank = i + 1;
        return `
          <div class="manifest-row" style="grid-template-columns:32px 1fr 80px 70px 70px 70px"
            onclick="Router.navigate('query');Panels.query.goHash('${m.hash}')">
            <div style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">${rank}</div>
            <div class="mr-hash">
              <span style="color:var(--text)">${e.architecture || '—'}</span>
              <span style="color:var(--text3);margin-left:8px">${fmt.params(e.parameter_count)}</span>
              <span style="color:var(--text3);margin-left:8px;font-size:10px">${e.connector_source || ''}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="mr-score ${scoreClass}">${fmt.score(m.score)}</div>
            <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);text-align:right">${m.attestation_count}</div>
            <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);text-align:right">${fmt.score(agentRep)}</div>
            <div class="hash" style="font-size:10px;text-align:right" onclick="event.stopPropagation();Router.navigate('query');Panels.query.goHash('${m.author}')">${fmt.hash(m.author)}</div>
          </div>
        `;
      }).join('');

      body.innerHTML = `
        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:32px 1fr 80px 70px 70px 70px;padding:8px 24px;font-size:9px;color:var(--text3);letter-spacing:0.1em;text-transform:uppercase;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)">
          <div>#</div><div>model</div><div style="text-align:right">score</div>
          <div style="text-align:right">att</div>
          <div style="text-align:right">agent rep</div>
          <div style="text-align:right">agent</div>
        </div>
        ${rows}
      `;
      this.loaded = true;
    } catch(e) {
      body.innerHTML = `<div class="empty">error: ${e.message}</div>`;
    }
  },
};

init();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Configuration
// Panels register themselves — adding a new panel
// requires only: add nav-item, add panel div, add
// to PANELS registry, implement render function.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
const apiPort = params.get('api') || '3000';
const API = `http://localhost:${apiPort}/v1`;
const SIGNALS_URL = `http://localhost:${apiPort}/signals`;

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// State
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const State = {
  agent: null,
  connected: false,
  networkState: null,
  reputation: null,
  myManifests: [],
  eventCount: 0,
};

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// API
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const Api = {
  async get(path) {
    const res = await fetch(`${API}${path}`);
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`${res.status} ${path}`);
    return res.json();
  },
  async post(path, body) {
    const res = await fetch(`${API}${path}`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify(body),
    });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`${res.status} ${path}`);
    return res.json();
  },
};

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Router
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const Router = {
  current: 'monitor',
  navigate(panelId) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(n => n.classList.remove('active'));
    const panel = document.getElementById(`panel-${panelId}`);
    const navItem = document.querySelector(`[data-panel="${panelId}"]`);
    if (panel) panel.classList.add('active');
    if (navItem) navItem.classList.add('active');
    this.current = panelId;
    Panels[panelId]?.onActivate?.();
  },
};

document.getElementById('nav').addEventListener('click', e => {
  const item = e.target.closest('.nav-item');
  if (item?.dataset.panel) Router.navigate(item.dataset.panel);
});

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Utilities
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const fmt = {
  hash: h => h ? `${h.slice(0,8)}…${h.slice(-6)}` : '—',
  score: s => typeof s === 'number' ? s.toFixed(4) : '—',
  delta: d => {
    if (typeof d !== 'number') return '';
    return d >= 0 ? `↑${d.toFixed(3)}` : `↓${Math.abs(d).toFixed(3)}`;
  },
  time: () => new Date().toISOString().slice(11, 19),
  arch: a => a || '—',
  params: n => {
    if (!n) return '—';
    if (n >= 1e12) return (n/1e12).toFixed(1)+'T';
    if (n >= 1e9)  return (n/1e9).toFixed(1)+'B';
    if (n >= 1e6)  return (n/1e6).toFixed(1)+'M';
    return n.toString();
  },
};

function copyText(text) {
  navigator.clipboard?.writeText(text).then(() => {
    const el = document.querySelector('.agent-key');
    if (el) {
      const orig = el.textContent;
      el.textContent = 'copied';
      el.style.color = 'var(--accent)';
      setTimeout(() => {
        el.textContent = orig;
        el.style.color = '';
      }, 300);
    }
  });
}

function passes(score) { return typeof score === 'number' && score >= 0.618; }

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Panels registry
// To add a new panel: implement { onActivate, render }
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

const Panels = {};

// ─── Monitor Panel ───────────────────────────────

let maxEvents = 200;

Panels.monitor = {
  onActivate() {},
  addEvent(type, hash, raw) {
    State.eventCount++;
    document.getElementById('sb-events').textContent = State.eventCount;

    const stream = document.getElementById('event-stream');
    const empty = stream.querySelector('.stream-empty');
    if (empty) empty.remove();

    const typeClass = {
      'ValidationRequested': 'validation',
      'QuorumReached':        'quorum',
      'AttestationCreated':   'attestation',
      'WarrantCreated':        'warrant',
      'ManifestCreated':       'manifest',
    }[type] || 'manifest';

    const typeLabel = {
      'ValidationRequested': 'VALIDATION.REQ',
      'QuorumReached':        'QUORUM.REACHED',
      'AttestationCreated':   'ATTESTATION',
      'WarrantCreated':        'WARRANT',
      'ManifestCreated':       'MANIFEST',
    }[type] || type;

    const row = document.createElement('div');
    row.className = 'event-row';
    row.innerHTML = `
      <span class="ev-time">${fmt.time()}</span>
      <span class="ev-type ${typeClass}">${typeLabel}</span>
      <span class="ev-hash">${hash || '—'}</span>
    `;

    stream.prepend(row);

    // Prune old events
    const rows = stream.querySelectorAll('.event-row');
    if (rows.length > maxEvents) rows[rows.length - 1].remove();
  },
};

// ─── Query Panel ─────────────────────────────────

Panels.query = {
  onActivate() {
    document.getElementById('search-input').focus();
  },
  async search(val) {
    const container = document.getElementById('query-result');
    container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty loading">querying</div>';

    try {
      if (val.startsWith('hCkk') || val.startsWith('hC')) {
        await this.renderManifest(container, val);
      } else if (val.startsWith('uhCAk') || val.startsWith('uhC')) {
        await this.renderAgent(container, val);
      } else if (val.startsWith('sha256:') || val.match(/^[a-f0-9]{64}$/)) {
        await this.renderConvergence(container, val);
      } else {
        container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">unrecognized format — enter manifest hash (hCkk...), agent pubkey (uhCAk...), or content hash (sha256:...)</div>';
      }
    } catch(e) {
      container.innerHTML = `<div class="empty">error: ${e.message}</div>`;
    }
  },

  async renderManifest(container, hash) {
    const entry_preview = await Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}`).catch(() => null);
    const contentHash = entry_preview?.entry?.content_hash;

    const [manifest, attestations, warrants, trustScore, upstreams, derivatives, convergenceHashes] = await Promise.all([
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}`),
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}/attestations`).catch(() => []),
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}/warrants`).catch(() => []),
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}/trust-score`).catch(() => null),
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}/upstreams`).catch(() => []),
      Api.get(`/manifest/${hash}/derivatives`).catch(() => []),
      contentHash ? Api.get(`/content/${encodeURIComponent(contentHash)}/manifests`).catch(() => []) : Promise.resolve([]),
    ]);

    const entry = manifest.entry || {};
    const score = trustScore?.score ?? 0;
    const pct = (score * 100).toFixed(1);
    const scoreClass = passes(score) ? 'accent' : 'warn';
    const warrantHtml = warrants.length > 0
      ? `<div class="warrant-banner">⚠ ${warrants.length} active warrant${warrants.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}</div>`
      : '';

    const attRows = (attestations || []).map(a => {
      const p = a.entry?.passed !== false;
      const sc = a.entry?.score != null ? Number(a.entry.score).toFixed(3) : '—';
      return `<div class="att-row">
        <div class="att-dot ${p ? 'pass' : 'fail'}"></div>
        <div class="att-agent hash" onclick="copyText('${a.author}')" title="${a.author}">${fmt.hash(a.author)}</div>
        <div class="att-score">${sc}</div>
        <div class="att-verdict ${p ? 'pass' : 'fail'}">${p ? 'pass' : 'fail'}</div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');

    const upstreamHtml = upstreams.length > 0
      ? upstreams.map(h => `<span class="lineage-hash" onclick="Panels.query.goHash('${h}')">${fmt.hash(h)}</span>`).join('')
      : '<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">none</span>';

    const derivHtml = derivatives.length > 0
      ? derivatives.map(h => `<span class="lineage-hash" onclick="Panels.query.goHash('${h}')">${fmt.hash(h)}</span>`).join('')
      : '<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">none</span>';

    container.innerHTML = `
      ${warrantHtml}
      <div class="query-result">
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header">
            <span class="rb-title">trust score</span>
            <span class="rb-value ${scoreClass}">${fmt.score(score)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="score-bar">
            <div class="score-fill ${passes(score) ? '' : 'warn'}" style="width:${pct}%"></div>
            <div class="score-threshold"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="kv-grid">
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">hash</div><div class="kv-val hash" onclick="copyText('${hash}')" title="${hash}">${fmt.hash(hash)}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">architecture</div><div class="kv-val">${fmt.arch(entry.architecture)}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">parameters</div><div class="kv-val">${fmt.params(entry.parameter_count)}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">version</div><div class="kv-val">${entry.version || '—'}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">source</div><div class="kv-val">${entry.connector_source || '—'}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">attestations</div><div class="kv-val ${attestations.length > 0 ? 'accent' : ''}">${attestations.length}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item" style="grid-column:1/-1"><div class="kv-key">description</div><div class="kv-val" style="white-space:normal">${entry.description || '—'}</div></div>
          </div>
        </div>

        ${attestations.length > 0 ? `
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header"><span class="rb-title">attestations</span></div>
          <div class="attestation-list">${attRows}</div>
        </div>` : ''}

        ${convergenceHashes.length > 1 ? `
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header">
            <span class="rb-title">convergence</span>
            <span class="rb-value accent">${convergenceHashes.length}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="lineage-section">
            <div class="lineage-label">independent registrations of same weights</div>
            <div>${convergenceHashes
              .filter(h => h !== hash)
              .map(h => `<span class="lineage-hash" onclick="Panels.query.goHash('${h}')">${fmt.hash(h)}</span>`)
              .join('')}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>` : ''}

        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header"><span class="rb-title">lineage</span></div>
          <div class="lineage-section">
            <div class="lineage-label">upstream</div>
            <div>${upstreamHtml}</div>
          </div>
          <div class="lineage-section" style="border-top:1px solid var(--border)">
            <div class="lineage-label">derivatives</div>
            <div>${derivHtml}</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  },

  async renderAgent(container, pubkey) {
    const [rep, manifests] = await Promise.all([
      Api.get(`/agent/${pubkey}/reputation`).catch(() => ({})),
      Api.get(`/agent/${pubkey}/manifests`).catch(() => []),
    ]);

    const deltaClass = rep.score_delta >= 0 ? 'up' : 'down';
    const manifestRows = manifests.map(m => {
      const e = m.entry || {};
      return `<div class="manifest-row" onclick="Panels.query.goHash('${m.hash}')">
        <div class="mr-hash hash">${fmt.hash(m.hash)} <span style="color:var(--text3)">${e.architecture || ''}</span></div>
        <div class="mr-arch">${fmt.params(e.parameter_count)}</div>
        <div class="mr-score">—</div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');

    container.innerHTML = `
      <div class="query-result">
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header">
            <span class="rb-title">agent</span>
            <span class="rb-value ${passes(rep.score) ? 'accent' : 'warn'}">${fmt.score(rep.score)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="kv-grid">
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">pubkey</div><div class="kv-val hash" onclick="copyText('${pubkey}')">${fmt.hash(pubkey)}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">trajectory</div><div class="kv-val ${deltaClass}">${fmt.delta(rep.score_delta)}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">attestations</div><div class="kv-val">${rep.attestation_count ?? 0}</div></div>
            <div class="kv-item"><div class="kv-key">warrants</div><div class="kv-val ${rep.warrant_count > 0 ? 'warn' : ''}">${rep.warrant_count ?? 0}</div></div>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${manifests.length > 0 ? `
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header"><span class="rb-title">manifests (${manifests.length})</span></div>
          ${manifestRows}
        </div>` : ''}
      </div>
    `;
  },

  async renderConvergence(container, contentHash) {
    const hashes = await Api.get(`/content/${encodeURIComponent(contentHash)}/manifests`).catch(() => []);
    container.innerHTML = `
      <div class="query-result">
        <div class="result-block">
          <div class="rb-header">
            <span class="rb-title">convergence</span>
            <span class="rb-value ${hashes.length > 1 ? 'accent' : 'neutral'}">${hashes.length}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="kv-grid">
            <div class="kv-item" style="grid-column:1/-1">
              <div class="kv-key">content hash</div>
              <div class="kv-val">${contentHash}</div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="lineage-section">
            <div class="lineage-label">independent registrations</div>
            <div>${hashes.length > 0
              ? hashes.map(h => `<span class="lineage-hash" onclick="Panels.query.goHash('${h}')">${fmt.hash(h)}</span>`).join('')
              : '<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">none found</span>'
            }</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  },

  goHash(hash) {
    document.getElementById('search-input').value = hash;
    this.search(hash);
  },
};

document.getElementById('search-input').addEventListener('keydown', e => {
  if (e.key === 'Enter') {
    const val = e.target.value.trim();
    if (val) Panels.query.search(val);
  }
});

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Signal Stream
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

function connectSignals() {
  const es = new EventSource(SIGNALS_URL);

  es.onmessage = (event) => {
    try {
      const signal = JSON.parse(event.data);
      const payload = signal?.value?.payload || signal;
      const type = payload?.type;
      if (!type) return;

      const hash =
        payload.request_hash ||
        payload.quorum_bundle_hash ||
        payload.action_hash || '';

      Panels.monitor.addEvent(type, fmt.hash(hash), payload);

      // Refresh network state quietly
      if (type === 'AttestationCreated' || type === 'QuorumReached') {
        Api.get('/network/state').then(s => {
          State.networkState = s;
          updateStatusBar(s);
        }).catch(() => {});
      }
    } catch(e) {}
  };

  es.onopen = () => {
    State.connected = true;
    updateConnectionStatus(true);
  };

  es.onerror = () => {
    State.connected = false;
    updateConnectionStatus(false);
    es.close();
    setTimeout(connectSignals, 5000);
  };
}

function updateConnectionStatus(connected) {
  const dot = document.getElementById('conn-dot');
  const label = document.getElementById('conn-status');
  dot.className = `status-dot${connected ? '' : ' offline'}`;
  label.textContent = connected ? 'connected' : 'reconnecting';
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Status bar
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

function updateStatusBar(state) {
  if (!state) return;
  document.getElementById('sb-att').textContent = state.attestation_count ?? '—';
  document.getElementById('sb-threshold').textContent = state.next_fibonacci_threshold ?? '—';
  document.getElementById('sb-supply').textContent = state.credit_supply?.toLocaleString() ?? '—';
  document.getElementById('sb-phase').textContent = state.phase === 0 ? 'genesis' : 'governed';
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Clock
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

function updateClock() {
  document.getElementById('tb-time').textContent = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,19).replace('T', ' ') + 'Z';
}
updateClock();
setInterval(updateClock, 1000);

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Init
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

async function init() {
  // Agent identity
  try {
    const { agent } = await Api.get('/agent/me');
    State.agent = agent;
    const keyEl = document.getElementById('agent-key');
    keyEl.textContent = fmt.hash(agent);
    keyEl.title = agent;
    keyEl.onclick = () => copyText(agent);
  } catch(e) {}

  // Network state
  try {
    const state = await Api.get('/network/state');
    State.networkState = state;
    updateStatusBar(state);
  } catch(e) {}

  // Signals
  connectSignals();

  // Poll network state every 10s
  setInterval(async () => {
    try {
      const s = await Api.get('/network/state');
      State.networkState = s;
      updateStatusBar(s);
    } catch(e) {}
  }, 10000);
}

Panels.browse = {
  loaded: false,
  async onActivate() {
    if (!this.loaded) await this.render();
  },
  async render() {
    const body = document.getElementById('browse-body');
    body.innerHTML = '<div class="empty loading">fetching manifests</div>';
    try {
      const manifests = await Api.get('/manifests');
      if (!manifests.length) {
        body.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">no manifests registered yet</div>';
        return;
      }

      // Fetch registering agent reputations
      const agentReps = {};
      await Promise.all([...new Set(manifests.map(m => m.author))].map(async a => {
        try {
          const rep = await Api.get(`/agent/${a}/reputation`);
          agentReps[a] = rep.score ?? 0;
        } catch(e) { agentReps[a] = 0; }
      }));

      const rows = manifests.map((m, i) => {
        const e = m.entry || {};
        const agentRep = agentReps[m.author] ?? 0;
        const scoreClass = m.passes ? 'pass' : '';
        const rank = i + 1;
        return `
          <div class="manifest-row" style="grid-template-columns:32px 1fr 80px 70px 70px 70px"
            onclick="Router.navigate('query');Panels.query.goHash('${m.hash}')">
            <div style="color:var(--text3);font-size:11px">${rank}</div>
            <div class="mr-hash">
              <span style="color:var(--text)">${e.architecture || '—'}</span>
              <span style="color:var(--text3);margin-left:8px">${fmt.params(e.parameter_count)}</span>
              <span style="color:var(--text3);margin-left:8px;font-size:10px">${e.connector_source || ''}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="mr-score ${scoreClass}">${fmt.score(m.score)}</div>
            <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);text-align:right">${m.attestation_count}</div>
            <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);text-align:right">${fmt.score(agentRep)}</div>
            <div class="hash" style="font-size:10px;text-align:right" onclick="event.stopPropagation();Router.navigate('query');Panels.query.goHash('${m.author}')">${fmt.hash(m.author)}</div>
          </div>
        `;
      }).join('');

      body.innerHTML = `
        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:32px 1fr 80px 70px 70px 70px;padding:8px 24px;font-size:9px;color:var(--text3);letter-spacing:0.1em;text-transform:uppercase;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)">
          <div>#</div><div>model</div><div style="text-align:right">score</div>
          <div style="text-align:right">att</div>
          <div style="text-align:right">agent rep</div>
          <div style="text-align:right">agent</div>
        </div>
        ${rows}
      `;
      this.loaded = true;
    } catch(e) {
      body.innerHTML = `<div class="empty">error: ${e.message}</div>`;
    }
  },
};

init();

/HOME/KITTY/PROJECTS/POI/VALIDATOR/INDEX.JS CODE IS BELOW
#!/usr/bin/env node
// Toric Validator Client v2
// Adds HuggingFace-aware hash verification.
// Auto-files warrants on hash mismatch — no manual path for tampered_weights.
// Usage: TORIC_AGENT=uhCAk... node index.js
// Dry run: DRY_RUN=true TORIC_AGENT=uhCAk... node index.js

import fetch from 'node-fetch';
import crypto from 'crypto';

const API           = process.env.TORIC_API    || process.env.POI_API    || 'http://localhost:3000';
const AGENT         = process.env.TORIC_AGENT  || process.env.POI_AGENT  || '';
const POLL_INTERVAL = parseInt(process.env.POLL_INTERVAL || '30000');
const DRY_RUN       = process.env.DRY_RUN === 'true';
const HF_TOKEN      = process.env.HF_TOKEN     || null;

console.log('Toric Validator Client v2');
console.log('API:', API);
console.log('Agent:', AGENT || '(not set)');
console.log('Poll interval:', POLL_INTERVAL + 'ms');
console.log('Dry run:', DRY_RUN);
console.log('HF token:', HF_TOKEN ? 'set' : 'not set (public models only)');
console.log('');

function toBase64url(hash) {
  if (!hash) return 'unknown';
  if (typeof hash === 'string') return hash.slice(0, 20) + '...';
  if (hash.type === 'Buffer') return Buffer.from(hash.data).toString('base64url').slice(0, 20) + '...';
  return 'unknown';
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
// HuggingFace helpers
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────

async function hfGet(path) {
  const headers = { 'Accept': 'application/json' };
  if (HF_TOKEN) headers['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${HF_TOKEN}`;
  const res = await fetch(`https://huggingface.co/api/${path}`, { headers });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HF API ${path} → ${res.status} ${res.statusText}`);
  return res.json();
}

function buildContentHash(siblings) {
  const weightExts = /\.(safetensors|bin|pt|gguf|ggml|pth|h5|ot)$/i;
  const weightFiles = siblings
    .filter(f => weightExts.test(f.rfilename) && f.lfs?.sha256)
    .sort((a, b) => a.rfilename.localeCompare(b.rfilename));

  if (weightFiles.length === 0) {
    const fallback = siblings
      .sort((a, b) => a.rfilename.localeCompare(b.rfilename))
      .map(f => `${f.rfilename}:${f.size || 0}`)
      .join('\n');
    return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(fallback).digest('hex');
  }

  const combined = weightFiles.map(f => f.lfs.sha256).join('\n');
  return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(combined).digest('hex');
}

function extractHfModelId(entry) {
  const tags = entry.tags || [];
  const tag = tags.find(t => t && t.startsWith('hf_id:'));
  return tag ? tag.slice(6) : null;
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
// Auto-warrant — fires when hash mismatch detected
// Evidence recorded first, severity computed by backend
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────

async function fileHashMismatchWarrant(manifestHash, registeredHash, computedHash) {
  if (DRY_RUN) {
    console.log('  [DRY RUN] would file TamperedWeights warrant');
    console.log('    registered:', registeredHash);
    console.log('    computed:  ', computedHash);
    return;
  }

  try {
    // Step 1 — record evidence (severity computed by backend: always 1_000_000 for hash mismatch)
    const evidenceRes = await fetch(`${API}/evidence`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        manifest_hash: manifestHash,
        evidence_type: 'hash_mismatch',
        expected: registeredHash,
        actual: computedHash,
        metadata: { validator: AGENT, detected_at: new Date().toISOString() },
      }),
    });
    const evidenceData = await evidenceRes.json();

    if (!evidenceData.hash) {
      console.log('  warrant evidence error:', evidenceData.error);
      return;
    }

    console.log('  evidence recorded:', evidenceData.hash.slice(0, 20) + '...');
    console.log('  computed severity:', evidenceData.computed_severity);

    // Step 2 — file warrant pointing at evidence
    const warrantRes = await fetch(`${API}/warrant`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        manifest_hash: manifestHash,
        blob: {
          blob_type: 'tampered_weights',
          evidence_hash: evidenceData.hash,
          expected_hash: registeredHash,
          found_hash: computedHash,
          computed_severity: evidenceData.computed_severity,
          description: `Hash mismatch detected by validator ${AGENT.slice(0, 20)}...`,
        },
      }),
    });
    const warrantData = await warrantRes.json();

    if (warrantData.hash) {
      console.log('  ⚠ warrant filed:', warrantData.hash.slice(0, 20) + '...');
    } else {
      console.log('  warrant error:', warrantData.error);
    }
  } catch(e) {
    console.log('  error filing warrant:', e.message);
  }
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
// Verify a manifest
// Returns { passed, score, details, mismatch }
// mismatch: { registered, computed } — set only on hash mismatch
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────

async function verifyManifest(manifest) {
  let entry = manifest.entry || {};
  const registeredHash = entry.content_hash;

  console.log('  registered hash:', registeredHash);

  if (!registeredHash) {
    return { passed: false, score: 0.0, details: 'No content_hash registered — cannot verify' };
  }

  const connectorSource = entry.connector_source;

  // Bittensor models that committed to HuggingFace — verify via HF
  if (connectorSource === 'bittensor') {
    const modelId = extractHfModelId(entry);
    if (modelId) {
      entry = { ...entry, connector_source: 'huggingface' };
    }
  }

  // ── HuggingFace path ──────────────────────
  if (connectorSource === 'huggingface' || entry.connector_source === 'huggingface') {
    const modelId = extractHfModelId(entry);

    if (!modelId) {
      console.log('  HF manifest but no hf_id tag — falling back to unverifiable');
      return {
        passed: true,
        score: 0.5,
        details: 'HuggingFace manifest — model ID not in tags, hash verification skipped',
      };
    }

    console.log('  HuggingFace model:', modelId);
    console.log('  fetching file list from HF API...');

    try {
      const info = await hfGet(`models/${modelId}`);
      const computedHash = buildContentHash(info.siblings || []);

      console.log('  computed hash: ', computedHash);
      const matches = computedHash === registeredHash;
      console.log('  match:', matches ? 'YES ✓' : 'NO ✗');

      if (matches) {
        const weightCount = (info.siblings || [])
          .filter(f => /\.(safetensors|bin|pt|gguf|ggml|pth|h5|ot)$/i.test(f.rfilename) && f.lfs?.sha256)
          .length;
        return {
          passed: true,
          score: 1.0,
          details: `HF hash verified: ${weightCount} weight files matched. Hash: ${computedHash}`,
        };
      } else {
        // Hash mismatch — return with mismatch data for auto-warrant
        return {
          passed: false,
          score: 0.0,
          details: `HF hash mismatch. Registered: ${registeredHash} | Recomputed: ${computedHash}`,
          mismatch: { registered: registeredHash, computed: computedHash },
        };
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.log('  HF API error:', e.message);
      return {
        passed: false,
        score: 0.0,
        details: `HF verification failed: ${e.message}`,
      };
    }
  }

  // ── Generic fallback ──
  console.log('  no verification path for connector_source:', connectorSource || 'none');
  return {
    passed: true,
    score: 0.5,
    details: `No verification method for connector_source="${connectorSource || 'none'}". Hash on record: ${registeredHash}`,
  };
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
// Parse request entry — extract manifest hash
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────

function extractManifestHash(request) {
  const entryBuf = request.entry?.Present?.entry;
  if (!entryBuf || entryBuf.type !== 'Buffer') return null;

  const data = Buffer.from(entryBuf.data);
  const keyMarker = Buffer.from([
    0xad,
    0x6d, 0x61, 0x6e, 0x69, 0x66, 0x65, 0x73, 0x74, 0x5f, 0x68, 0x61, 0x73, 0x68,
  ]);
  const keyIdx = data.indexOf(keyMarker);
  if (keyIdx === -1) return null;

  const hashStart = keyIdx + keyMarker.length + 2;
  const hashBytes = data.slice(hashStart, hashStart + 39);
  return hashBytes.toString('base64url');
}

function extractRequestHash(request) {
  const hashBuf = request.signed_action?.hashed?.hash;
  if (!hashBuf || hashBuf.type !== 'Buffer') return null;
  return Buffer.from(hashBuf.data).toString('base64url');
}

async function processRequest(request, agent) {
  const requestHash = extractRequestHash(request);
  if (!requestHash) { console.log('  skipping — cannot parse request hash'); return; }

  console.log('  processing:', requestHash.slice(0, 30) + '...');

  // Skip if quorum already reached
  try {
    const qRes = await fetch(`${API}/validation/quorum`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ request_hash: requestHash }),
    });
    const qData = await qRes.json();
    if (qData.reached) {
      console.log('  quorum already reached — skipping');
      return;
    }
  } catch(e) { /* proceed if check fails */ }

  const manifestHash = extractManifestHash(request);
  if (!manifestHash) { console.log('  skipping — cannot parse manifest hash'); return; }

  console.log('  manifest hash:', manifestHash.slice(0, 30) + '...');

  let manifest;
  try {
    const res = await fetch(`${API}/manifest/${manifestHash}`);
    if (!res.ok) { console.log('  manifest not found'); return; }
    manifest = await res.json();
  } catch(e) {
    console.log('  error fetching manifest:', e.message);
    return;
  }

  const entry = manifest.entry || {};
  console.log('  connector_source:', entry.connector_source || 'none');

  const result = await verifyManifest(manifest);
  console.log('  verdict:', result.passed ? 'PASS ✓' : 'FAIL ✗');
  console.log('  score:', result.score);

  // Auto-file warrant on hash mismatch — no manual path for this type
  if (result.mismatch) {
    console.log('  hash mismatch detected — filing warrant automatically...');
    await fileHashMismatchWarrant(
      manifestHash,
      result.mismatch.registered,
      result.mismatch.computed
    );
  }

  if (DRY_RUN) {
    console.log('  [DRY RUN] skipping submission');
    return;
  }

  // Phase 1 — commit
  const salt = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
  const preimage = `${result.passed}:${result.score}:${result.details || ''}:${salt}`;
  const commitmentHash = crypto.createHash('sha256').update(preimage).digest('hex');

  console.log('  committing...');
  try {
    const commitRes = await fetch(`${API}/validation/commit`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        request_hash: requestHash,
        commitment_hash: commitmentHash,
      }),
    });
    const commitData = await commitRes.json();
    if (!commitData.hash) {
      console.log('  commit error:', commitData.error);
      return;
    }
    console.log('  committed:', commitData.hash.slice(0, 20) + '...');
  } catch(e) {
    console.log('  error committing:', e.message);
    return;
  }

  // Wait for reveal window — poll until φ⁴ threshold crossed
  console.log('  waiting for reveal window...');
  let windowOpen = false;
  for (let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 3000));
    try {
      const windowRes = await fetch(`${API}/validation/reveal-window`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ request_hash: requestHash }),
      });
      const windowData = await windowRes.json();
      console.log(`  reveal window: ${windowData.reveal_window_open ? 'OPEN' : 'waiting'} (weight ${windowData.commitment_weight?.toFixed(3)}, threshold ${windowData.phi_4_threshold?.toFixed(3)})`);
      if (windowData.reveal_window_open) {
        windowOpen = true;
        break;
      }
    } catch(e) { /* continue polling */ }
  }

  if (!windowOpen) {
    console.log('  reveal window did not open after 30s — will retry next poll');
    return;
  }

  // Phase 2 — reveal
  console.log('  revealing...');
  try {
    const revealRes = await fetch(`${API}/validation/reveal`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        request_hash: requestHash,
        passed: result.passed,
        score: result.score,
        details: result.details,
        salt,
      }),
    });
    const revealData = await revealRes.json();
    if (revealData.hash) console.log('  revealed:', revealData.hash.slice(0, 20) + '...');
    else console.log('  reveal error:', revealData.error);
  } catch(e) {
    console.log('  error revealing:', e.message);
  }
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────
// Main validation loop
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────

async function runValidationCycle(agent) {
  console.log('[' + new Date().toISOString() + '] checking for pending requests...');
  try {
    const res = await fetch(`${API}/validation/pending/${agent}`);
    const requests = await res.json();

    if (!requests || requests.length === 0) {
      console.log('  no pending requests');
      return;
    }

    console.log('  found', requests.length, 'pending request(s)');
    for (const request of requests) {
      await processRequest(request, agent);
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1000));
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.log('  error:', e.message);
  }
}

async function start() {
  if (!AGENT) {
    console.error('TORIC_AGENT environment variable required.');
    process.exit(1);
  }

  console.log('Starting validator for agent:', AGENT);
  console.log('');

// Register agent identity on startup
  try {
    const softwareHash = crypto.createHash('sha256')
      .update(process.version + 'toric-validator-v2')
      .digest('hex');
    const regRes = await fetch(`${API}/agent/register`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        agent_type: 'validator',
        capabilities: ['validate:hash'],
        software_hash: softwareHash,
        version: '2.0.0',
        metadata: { started_at: new Date().toISOString() },
      }),
    });
    const regData = await regRes.json();
    if (regData.hash) console.log('Agent registered:', regData.hash.slice(0, 20) + '...');
    else console.log('Agent registration:', regData.error || 'already registered');
  } catch(e) {
    console.log('Agent registration failed (non-fatal):', e.message);
  }

  // Run initial poll
  await runValidationCycle(AGENT);

  // Subscribe to signals for real-time notification
  subscribeToSignals(AGENT);

  // Fallback poll every 5 minutes — signals handle liveness
  setInterval(() => runValidationCycle(AGENT), 300000);
}

async function subscribeToSignals(agent) {
  console.log('Subscribing to signal stream...');
  const EventSourceModule = await import('eventsource');
  const EventSource = EventSourceModule.default || EventSourceModule.EventSource || EventSourceModule;

  function connect() {
    const es = new EventSource(`${API}/signals`);

    es.onmessage = async (event) => {
      try {
        const signal = JSON.parse(event.data);
        const payload = signal?.value?.payload || signal;
        if (payload?.type === 'ValidationRequested') {
          console.log('[signal] ValidationRequested:', toBase64url(payload.request_hash));
          await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 2000));
          await runValidationCycle(agent);
        }
      } catch(e) {
        console.log('signal parse error:', e.message);
      }
    };

    es.onerror = () => {
      console.log('Signal stream disconnected — reconnecting in 5s...');
      es.close();
      setTimeout(connect, 5000);
    };

    console.log('Signal stream connected');
  }

  connect();
}

start();
